 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

  )

    (visited kitchen)

    (door kitchen patio-unknown west)

 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

  )

    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)

                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))

 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

Parsed df and pf: 
 (define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain home-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?l - location)
    (visited ?l - location)
    (connected ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
    :effect (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir)
                       (or (not (door ?from ?to ?dir)) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)
